<review>I traveled to the Stage Stop to do a private party transfer. It was about a 40 minute drive and it turned out to be well worth it. They actually had a good selection of guns with a solid inventory of parts accessories and ammo. I completed my transfer and took a closer look at there Henry rifles. I found the exact model I have been looking for. which I would have had to order from one of my local shops. Their price was fair, i just got cash for my transferred gun so i squeezed the trigger. In addition they had some Savage magazines that  I wanted in stock, some trigger expanders for my single action revolvers and 17HMR ammo at a decent price.  Their salesman started my paperwork as another salesman was finishing up the transfer forms with the buyer. This enabled me to complete both transactions at the same time. In conclusion, their service was top notch. The inventory was excellent for the current situation we are now dealing with. I will be returning to the Stage Stop for any future gun consideration as they deserve it.  Well done.<//review><Gmap_id>0x80916b9d54b260bf:0xb48e6180cdfc7d4f< /Gmap_id><date>1605607331260</date>< Rate>

They were informed of this mistake immediately and today, 2weeks later they finally sent new closing disclosures with no correction to their egregious errors. BTW, I am also in escrow on a house.  The proceeds from the sale of my condo are to be used for the down payment on my house.  As a result of their errors, and slow response to make corrections I have now incurred additional fees to extend the rate lock on the purchase of my house.  I am deeply disappointed with the complete incompetence displayed on the part of Motive Lending and their associates.   As it stands now if they don't make these corrections, between my rate lock extension and the 1.83 Points I will incurr additional costs of around $5700.  We still have yet to complete this transaction so I can't say they won't right their wrongs. If I could give 10 stars, I would. I've ate at plenty of restaurants that knock you back into your seat and make you question all your previous food choices, but this place may, hands down, have been the best food I've ever had, and I'm close with a few top-end chefs in Colorado. Also, I consider myself a bit of a Mexican food connoisseur and chef, and still... Man, it was unbelievably good...

Everything about my dish was perfect. Each ingredient was cooked with the best method to it's optimal temperature separately and then combined when appropriate. This was truly gourmet tasting food in a small, husband-wife combo ran Mexican restaurant.

ON TOP OF THAT, the service was PHENOMENAL. I swear our waitress had to love her job, because she was incredible and we thoroughly enjoyed her company.</Review>

< text>
When things go according to plan, it is easy to give 5 stars, but the true test of a company is the authority it gives to their employees to do the right thing and fix an unplanned situation for the customer.  Here's what happened...

I had a GREAT experience with RV&AP and if you get an opportunity to work with Crystal, you will wish for 6 stars to rate her here!  My order came earlier than expected, but the box was torn open during shipping and it was missing two key parts.  I called Crystal, she sent a return-ship request (free to me) and then sent me a replacement.  The replacement came unharmed and I installed the Reese Puck system on my F-250.

While the first box did not come as planned, the key here is that it was not RV&AP's fault, but they did right by me and fixed the situation in a timely manner.  THAT is how a GREAT company operates!

Robert Jimenez-McWilliams is with Juan Jimenez-McWilliams and Griselda Celis.
Just now ¬∑
DELICIOUS!!!! The Restaurant "Taqueria El Guero, Authentic Mexican Food" and it truly is. This place is a Hidden Gem in the Stater Brothers Plaza in the Far Right Corner. You would hardly know it's there, But!!! you need to know its there!!! The food there is out of this world. So many choices to choose from, and each one made to perfection. I had the Shrimp Fajita and I could not stop eating it. The Owner, Chuy, is also the cook and great personality and our server Griselda Celis speaks Spanish and English and is so friendly and helpful. Great Owner, Great Staff and Fantastic food as you can see in my photos, what more can you ask for. This is a Must Go To Place in Desert Hot Springs. !!!
Address is: 13-156 Palm Drive, Desert Hot Springs.< /Review>< Pics>
